      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geology">
        Geology
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mediterranean_Sea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Geology">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>
          </a>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This section
          <b>
           needs additional citations for
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">
            verification
           </a>
          </b>
          .
          <span class="hide-when-compact">
           Please help
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mediterranean_Sea&amp;action=edit">
            improve this article
           </a>
           by
           <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">
            adding citations to reliable sources
           </a>
           . Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.
          </span>
          <small>
           <i>
            (May 2012)
           </i>
          </small>
          <small class="hide-when-compact">
           <i>
            (
            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">
             Learn how and when to remove this template message
            </a>
            )
           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Geology_and_paleoclimatology_of_the_Mediterranean_Basin" title="Geology and paleoclimatology of the Mediterranean Basin">
        Geology and paleoclimatology of the Mediterranean Basin
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="1200" height="225" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg/300px-Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg/450px-Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg/600px-Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vrulja_kod_Omi%C5%A1a.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A submarine
         <a href="/wiki/Karst_spring" title="Karst spring">
          karst spring
         </a>
         , called
         <i>
          vrulja
         </i>
         , near
         <a href="/wiki/Omi%C5%A1" title="Omiš">
          Omiš
         </a>
         ; observed through several ripplings of an otherwise calm sea surface.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Geology" title="Geology">
        geologic history
       </a>
       of the Mediterranean Sea is complex. Underlain by
       <a href="/wiki/Oceanic_crust" title="Oceanic crust">
        oceanic crust
       </a>
       , the sea basin was once thought to be a tectonic remnant of the ancient
       <a href="/wiki/Tethys_Ocean" title="Tethys Ocean">
        Tethys Ocean
       </a>
       ; it is now known to be a structurally younger basin, called the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Neotethys" title="Neotethys">
        Neotethys
       </a>
       , which was first formed by the convergence of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_plate" title="African plate">
        African
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eurasian_plate" title="Eurasian plate">
        Eurasian plates
       </a>
       during the Late
       <a href="/wiki/Triassic" title="Triassic">
        Triassic
       </a>
       and Early
       <a href="/wiki/Jurassic" title="Jurassic">
        Jurassic
       </a>
       . Because it is a near-landlocked body of water in a normally dry climate, the Mediterranean is subject to intensive evaporation and the precipitation of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evaporites" title="Evaporites">
        evaporites
       </a>
       . The
       <a href="/wiki/Messinian_salinity_crisis" title="Messinian salinity crisis">
        Messinian salinity crisis
       </a>
       started about six million years ago (mya) when the Mediterranean became landlocked, and then essentially dried up. There are salt deposits accumulated on the bottom of the basin of more than a million cubic kilometres—in some places more than three kilometres thick.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         [42]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
        <a href="#cite_note-43">
         [43]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Scientists estimate that the sea was last filled about 5.3 million years ago (mya) in less than two years by the
       <a href="/wiki/Zanclean_flood" title="Zanclean flood">
        Zanclean flood
       </a>
       . Water poured in from the Atlantic Ocean through a newly breached gateway now called the
       <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Gibraltar" title="Strait of Gibraltar">
        Strait of Gibraltar
       </a>
       at an estimated rate of about three orders of magnitude (one thousand times) larger than the current flow of the
       <a href="/wiki/Amazon_River" title="Amazon River">
        Amazon River
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GCetal2009_44-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-GCetal2009-44">
         [44]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The Mediterranean Sea has an average depth of 1,500 m (4,900 ft) and the deepest recorded point is 5,267 m (17,280 ft) in the
       <a href="/wiki/Calypso_Deep" title="Calypso Deep">
        Calypso Deep
       </a>
       in the
       <a href="/wiki/Ionian_Sea" title="Ionian Sea">
        Ionian Sea
       </a>
       . The coastline extends for 46,000 km (29,000 mi). A shallow submarine ridge (the
       <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Sicily" title="Strait of Sicily">
        Strait of Sicily
       </a>
       ) between the island of
       <a href="/wiki/Sicily" title="Sicily">
        Sicily
       </a>
       and the coast of
       <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">
        Tunisia
       </a>
       divides the sea in two main subregions: the Western Mediterranean, with an area of about 850 thousand km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (330 thousand mi
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       ); and the Eastern Mediterranean, of about 1.65 million km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (640 thousand mi
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       ). A characteristic of the coastal Mediterranean are submarine
       <a href="/wiki/Karst_spring" title="Karst spring">
        karst springs
       </a>
       or
       <i>
        <span lang="hr" xml:lang="hr">
         <i>
          vrulja
         </i>
        </span>
       </i>
       s, which discharge pressurised groundwater into the coastal seawater from below the surface; the discharge water is usually fresh, and sometimes may be thermal.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LaMoreaux2001_45-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-LaMoreaux2001-45">
         [45]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
        <a href="#cite_note-46">
         [46]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tectonics_and_paleoenvironmental_analysis">
        Tectonics and paleoenvironmental analysis
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mediterranean_Sea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Tectonics and paleoenvironmental analysis">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:332px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Etapa3muda.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2195" data-file-width="3246" height="223" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Etapa3muda.jpg/330px-Etapa3muda.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Etapa3muda.jpg/495px-Etapa3muda.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Etapa3muda.jpg/660px-Etapa3muda.jpg 2x" width="330"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Etapa3muda.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Messinian salinity crisis before the
         <a href="/wiki/Zanclean_flood" title="Zanclean flood">
          Zanclean flood
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:332px;">
        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_0" style="width:330px;" videopayload='&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:640px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_1" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Crisis_salina_del_Messiniense.ogv/640px--Crisis_salina_del_Messiniense.ogv.jpg" controls="" preload="none" autoplay="" style="width:640px;height:480px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="74.112" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Crisis_salina_del_Messiniense.ogv" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/2/2e/Crisis_salina_del_Messiniense.ogv/Crisis_salina_del_Messiniense.ogv.480p.webm" type="video/webm;
